We may also collect information about how your device has interacted with our Website, including the pages accessed and links clicked.<br/><br/>Collecting this information enables us to better understand the visitors who come to our Website, where they come from, and what content on our Website is of interest to them. We use this information for our internal analytics purposes and to improve the quality and relevance of our Website to our visitors.<br/><br/>If you arrange a call with one of our sales team the call will be recorded using Gong for the purposes of training and learning. You can request that the recording be stopped and not retained at any point during the call.<br/><br/>Some of this information may be collected using cookies and similar tracking technology, as explained further in our <a class="link-component styled" href="/cookie-statement/">Cookie Statement</a>.</div></li><li class="ListItem-module--ul-marker--30352 markdown-li"><div party sources (including from companies that provide marketing lead information), but only where we have checked that these third parties either have your consent or are otherwise legally permitted or required to disclose your personal information to us.<br/><br/>The types of information we collect from third parties include your name and contact information and we use the information we receive To make such a request, or to opt out of such email advertisements or third-party disclosures, please send an email to <a rel="noopener noreferrer" class="link-component styled" href="mailto:DPO@singlestore.com" target="_blank">DPO@singlestore.com</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="page-container hr-component padding-small"><hr class="hr"/></div><span class="anchor-component with-subnav" id="security"></span><div class="section-container modular-page-sections-component section-generic-template size-medium overlay-top-none"><div class="content"><div class="page-container padding-small"><div class="margin-component bottom-small-x"><h2 class="typography-title h2 with-anchor">Security<a class="anchor-link-component title-anchor-link" href="#security"><svg aria-labelledby="svg-inline--fa-title-identical-id" data-prefix="fasr" data-icon="link" class="svg-inline--fa fa-link icon-component" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 640 512"><title id="svg-inline--fa-title-identical-id">security</title><path fill="currentColor" d="M59.7 244.8C3.5 301 3.5 392.1 59.7 448.2c53.6 53.6 139.5 56.4 196.5 6.5l6.1-5.4-31.6-36.1-6.1 5.4c-38 33.2-95.2 31.3-130.9-4.4c-37.4-37.4-37.4-98.1 0-135.6L207 165.4c37.4-37.4 98.1-37.4 135.6 0c35.7 35.7 37.6 92.9 4.4 130.9l-5.4 6.1L377.7 334l5.4-6.1c49.9-57 47-142.9-6.5-196.5c-56.2-56.2-147.3-56.2-203.5 0L59.7 244.8zm520.6 22.4c56.2-56.2 56.2-147.3 0-203.5C526.8 10.2 440.9 7.3 383.9 57.2l-6.1 5.4 31.6 36.1 6.1-5.4c38-33.2 95.2-31.3 130.9 4.4c37.4 37.4 37.4 98.1 0 135.6L433.1 346.6c-37.4 37.4-98.2 37.4-135.6 0c-35.7-35.7-37.6-92.9-4.4-130.9l4.7-5.4-36.1-31.6-4.7 5.4c-49.8 57-46.9 142.9 6.6 196.4c56.2 56.2 147.3 56.2 203.5 0L580.3 267.2z"></path></svg></a></h2></div></div><div class="page-container padding-small"><div class="columns"><div class="modular-text-component p1 regular column"><p class="typography-text p1-normal">Security of all information is of the utmost importance for SingleStore. We use technical and physical safeguards, including industry-standard encryption technology, to protect the security of your personal information from unauthorized disclosure. We also take reasonable efforts to ensure that only authorized people and third parties have access to personal information. Nevertheless, no service is completely secure and security measures cannot prevent all loss, misuse or alteration of personal information; we are not responsible for any damages or liabilities relating to any such incidents to the fullest extent permitted by law. Where required under law, we will notify you of any such loss, misuse or alteration of personal information that may affect you so that you can take the appropriate actions for the protection of your rights. SingleStore also reviews its security procedures periodically to consider appropriate new technology and updated methods.</p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">We also require that our third party service providers and channel partners agree to keep all information we share with them confidential, and to use the information only to perform their obligations pursuant to the agreements we have in place with them. These third party service providers and channel partners are expected to maintain privacy and security protections that are consistent with SingleStore’s privacy and information security policies. While we provide these third parties with no more information than is necessary to perform the function for which we engaged them, any information that you provide to these third parties independently of SingleStore is subject to their respective privacy policies and practices.</p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">Overall, SingleStore is committed to information security and is audited by accredited and independent third parties for that effect. More information about our current certifications can be found at <a class="link-component styled" href="/security/">singlestore.com/security</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="page-container hr-component padding-small"><hr class="hr"/></div><span class="anchor-component with-subnav" id="changes-to-this-notice"></span><div class="section-container modular-page-sections-component section-generic-template size-medium overlay-top-none"><div class="content"><div class="page-container padding-small"><div class="margin-component bottom-small-x"><h2 class="typography-title h2 with-anchor">Changes to This Notice<a class="anchor-link-component title-anchor-link" href="#changes-to-this-notice"><svg aria-labelledby="svg-inline--fa-title-identical-id" data-prefix="fasr" data-icon="link" class="svg-inline--fa fa-link icon-component" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 640 512"><title id="svg-inline--fa-title-identical-id">changes-to-this-notice</title><path fill="currentColor" d="M59.7 244.8C3.5 301 3.5 392.1 59.7 448.2c53.6 53.6 139.5 56.4 196.5 6.5l6.1-5.4-31.6-36.1-6.1 5.4c-38 33.2-95.2 31.3-130.9-4.4c-37.4-37.4-37.4-98.1 0-135.6L207 165.4c37.4-37.4 98.1-37.4 135.6 0c35.7 35.7 37.6 92.9 4.4 130.9l-5.4 6.1L377.7 334l5.4-6.1c49.9-57 47-142.9-6.5-196.5c-56.2-56.2-147.3-56.2-203.5 0L59.7 244.8zm520.6 22.4c56.2-56.2 56.2-147.3 0-203.5C526.8 10.2 440.9 7.3 383.9 57.2l-6.1 5.4 31.6 36.1 6.1-5.4c38-33.2 95.2-31.3 130.9 4.4c37.4 37.4 37.4 98.1 0 135.6L433.1 346.6c-37.4 37.4-98.2 37.4-135.6 0c-35.7-35.7-37.6-92.9-4.4-130.9l4.7-5.4-36.1-31.6-4.7 5.4c-49.8 57-46.9 142.9 6.6 196.4c56.2 56.2 147.3 56.2 203.5 0L580.3 267.2z"></path></svg></a></h2></div></div><div class="page-container padding-small"><div class="columns"><div class="modular-text-component p1 regular column"><p class="typography-text p1-normal">SingleStore may change this Privacy Notice from time to time. These rights include the following:</span></p><ol class="List-module--list-component--d72f9 markdown-list markdown-ol"><li class="markdown-li"><div class="typography-text p1-normal markdown-text"><p class="typography-text p1-normal"><strong>Notice at Collection</strong></p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">At or before the time of collection, you have a right to receive notice of our practices, including the categories of personal information and sensitive personal information to be <a class="anchor-link-component link-component styled" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="#personal-information">collected</a>, the <a class="anchor-link-component link-component styled" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="#business-or-commercial">purposes</a> for which such information is collected or used, whether such information is <a class="anchor-link-component link-component styled" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="#your-rights-and-choices">sold or shared</a>, and how long such information is <a rel="noopener noreferrer" class="link-component styled" href="https://www.singlestore.com/privacy-notice/#data-retention">retained</a>. You can find those details in this notice by clicking on the above links.</p></div></li><li class="markdown-li"><div class="typography-text p1-normal markdown-text"><p class="typography-text p1-normal"><strong>Right to opt out of “selling” or “sharing” certain Personal Information</strong></p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">You have a right to opt-out from future “sales” or “sharing” of personal information as those terms are defined by the CCPA.Note that we do not “sell” or “share” personal information as defined by the CCPA and have not done so in the past 12 months.</p></div></li><li class="markdown-li"><div class="typography-text p1-normal markdown-text"><p class="typography-text p1-normal"><strong>Right to Know</strong></p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">You have a right to request that we disclose to you the personal information we have collected about you. You also have a right to request additional information about our collection, use, disclosure, or sale of such personal information. Note that we have provided much of this information in this privacy notice.</p></div></li><li class="markdown-li"><div class="typography-text p1-normal markdown-text"><p class="typography-text p1-normal"><strong>Right to Request Correction</strong></p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">You have a right to request correction of inaccurate personal information.</p></div></li><li class="markdown-li"><div class="typography-text p1-normal markdown-text"><p class="typography-text p1-normal"><strong>Right to Request Deletion</strong></p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">You have a right to request that we delete personal information under certain circumstances, subject to certain exceptions.</p></div></li><li class="markdown-li"><div class="typography-text p1-normal markdown-text"><p class="typography-text p1-normal"><strong>Right to Limit Use and Disclosure of Sensitive Personal Information</strong></p><p class="typography-text p1-normal">You have a right to limit our use of sensitive personal information for any purposes other than to provide the services or goods you request or as otherwise permitted by law.
